\DoxyCodeLine{00087\ \ \ \ \ V4L2\_FIELD\_ANY\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 0,\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ driver\ can\ choose\ from\ none,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00088\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ top,\ bottom,\ interlaced}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00089\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ depending\ on\ whatever\ it\ thinks}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00091\ \ \ \ \ V4L2\_FIELD\_NONE\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1,\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ this\ device\ has\ no\ fields\ ...\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00092\ \ \ \ \ V4L2\_FIELD\_TOP\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 2,\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ top\ field\ only\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00093\ \ \ \ \ V4L2\_FIELD\_BOTTOM\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 3,\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ bottom\ field\ only\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00094\ \ \ \ \ V4L2\_FIELD\_INTERLACED\ \ \ \ =\ 4,\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ both\ fields\ interlaced\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00095\ \ \ \ \ V4L2\_FIELD\_SEQ\_TB\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 5,\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ both\ fields\ sequential\ into\ one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00096\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ buffer,\ top-\/bottom\ order\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00097\ \ \ \ \ V4L2\_FIELD\_SEQ\_BT\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 6,\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ same\ as\ above\ +\ bottom-\/top\ order\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00098\ \ \ \ \ V4L2\_FIELD\_ALTERNATE\ \ \ \ \ =\ 7,\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ both\ fields\ alternating\ into}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00099\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ separate\ buffers\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00100\ \ \ \ \ V4L2\_FIELD\_INTERLACED\_TB\ =\ 8,\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ both\ fields\ interlaced,\ top\ field}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00101\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ first\ and\ the\ top\ field\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00102\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ transmitted\ first\ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00105\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ transmitted\ first\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00106\ \};}

\DoxyCodeLine{01553\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01554\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ CEA-\/861\ specific:\ only\ valid\ for\ video\ transmitters,\ the\ flag\ is\ cleared}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01555\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ by\ receivers.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01556\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ If\ the\ framerate\ of\ the\ format\ is\ a\ multiple\ of\ six,\ then\ the\ pixelclock}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01557\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ used\ to\ set\ up\ the\ transmitter\ is\ divided\ by\ 1.001\ to\ make\ it\ compatible}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01558\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ with\ 60\ Hz\ based\ standards\ such\ as\ NTSC\ and\ PAL-\/M\ that\ use\ a\ framerate\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01559\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ 29.97\ Hz.\ Otherwise\ this\ flag\ is\ cleared.\ If\ the\ transmitter\ can't\ generate}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01561\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
